Black Clover (TV)

Have you seen this? want to / seen some / seen all

[ adapted from Black Clover (manga) ]

Related anime:
Black Clover: Sword of the Wizard King (movie)
Mugyutto! Black Clover (ONA) (spinoff)

Alternative title:
ブラッククローバー (Japanese)
黑色四叶草 (Chinese (PRC))
Genres: action, comedy, fantasy
Themes: elemental magic
find similar anime based on genres & themes
Objectionable content: Significant
Plot Summary: Asta is a young boy who dreams of becoming the greatest mage in the kingdom. He only has one problem, he can't use magic. Luckily for Asta, he receives the incredibly rare five-leaf clover grimoire that gives him the power of anti-magic. Even though he can't use magic, he plans to become the Wizard King. (from manga)
Watch Black Clover on: Apple TV, Google Play Movies, Amazon Video, Netflix, Hulu, Crunchyroll, Netflix basic with Ads, Crunchyroll Amazon Channel,

Yokusaru Shibata's Tojima Tanzaburo wa Kamen Rider ni Naritai Manga Gets Anime

Mar 7, 09:42
3 comments
manga anime
Series from Air Master manga creator about 40-year-old man who dreams of becoming a Kamen Rider launched in 2018 ― Aniplex announced on Friday that Yokusaru Shibata's Tojima Tanzaburo wa Kamen Rider ni Naritai (Tanzaburo Tojima Wants to Be a Kamen Rider) manga is getting an anime adaptation. The logo for the anime lists the title in English as Tojima Tanzaburo Wants to be a Masked Rider. Shibata drew...
